<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 10pt; margin: 0pt; text-align: left">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 9pt; text-indent: 36pt;">On June 6, 2025, we entered into a Securities Purchase Agreement, dated as of June 5, 2025, with certain accredited investors (the &#8220;2025 Purchase Agreement&#8221;), pursuant to which we issued and sold, in a private placement (the &#8220;2025 Private Placement&#8221;), Pre-Funded Warrants&nbsp;to acquire up to 1,989,392&nbsp;shares of our Common Stock in exchange for gross proceeds of approximately $7,500,000. In connection with the 2025 Private Placement, we also issued 2025 Placement Agent Warrants to acquire up to 99,470&nbsp;shares of our Common Stock,&nbsp;in consideration for services provided thereto.&nbsp;We have also issued an Advisor Warrant to acquire up to 100,000 shares of our Common Stock&nbsp;to Brandon Sofer, our advisory agent (in such capacity, the "Advisory Agent") in connection with the Advisory Agent's provision of certain treasury advisory services. We were required pursuant to the terms of the 2025 Purchase Agreement to file a registration statement registering the shares of Common Stock issuable upon the exercise of the Pre-Funded Warrants within 15 days of the date of the 2025 Purchase Agreement and we are required pursuant to the terms of the Advisory Agent Agreement, dated June 5, 2025, between the Company and the Advisory Agent, to register the shares of Common Stock issuable upon the exercise of the Advisor Warrants within 90 days of the issuance of the Advisor Warrants.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 9pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;">On March 30, 2023, Oblong, Inc. (&#8220;we&#8221; or the &#8220;Company&#8221;) entered into the 2023&nbsp;Securities Purchase Agreement with certain accredited investors (the &#8220;Investors&#8221;), pursuant to which we issued and sold, in a private placement transaction (the &#8220;2023 Private Placement&#8221;) (i) 6,550 shares of Series F Preferred Stock (the &#8220;Preferred Shares&#8221;), (ii) warrants to acquire up to 32,750 shares of Series F Preferred Stock, and (iii) common warrants to acquire up to 1,918,371 shares of Common Stock&nbsp;in exchange for&nbsp;gross proceeds of approximately $6,386,000. In connection with the 2023&nbsp;Private Placement, we also issued 2023&nbsp;Placement Agent Warrants to acquire up to 153,470 shares of our Common Stock,&nbsp;in consideration for services provided thereto.&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;">On August 23, 2024, the Company effected a 1-for-40 reverse stock split of its Common Stock (the &#8220;Reverse Stock Split&#8221;). All Common Stock share information through&nbsp;this prospectus is shown as adjusted for this stock&nbsp;split retrospectively for all periods represented herein.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 9pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 36pt;">From the closing date of the 2023 Private Placement through <a data-tblloc="2x2" data-tblname="723163" data-tblv="20" id="led723163F20256171752763454278">July 15, 2025</a>, the Company has: i)&nbsp;issued&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="1x1" data-tblname="723595" data-tblv="20" id="led723595F20256171752777365890">1,923</a> Preferred Shares&nbsp;and&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="5x1" data-tblname="723595" data-tblv="20" id="led723595F20256171752777552132">558,383</a> Common Warrants&nbsp;in accordance with the exercise provisions&nbsp;of&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="1x1" data-tblname="723595" data-tblv="20" id="led723595F20256171752777564742">1,923</a> Preferred Stock Warrants; ii) converted&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x1" data-tblname="723595" data-tblv="20" id="led723595F20256171752777575706">8,273</a> Preferred Shares, plus accrued dividends of approximately <a data-tblloc="4x2" data-tblname="723595" data-tblv="20" id="led723595F20256171752777594599">$436,000</a>, into&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="3x1" data-tblname="723595" data-tblv="20" id="led723595F20256171752777614649">804,959</a> shares of Common Stock; and iii) issued&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="0x1" data-tblname="723595" data-tblv="20" id="led723595F20256171752777634540">804,039</a> shares of Common Stock pursuant to the exercise of&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="0x1" data-tblname="723595" data-tblv="20" id="led723595F20256171752777640561">804,039</a> Common Warrants.&nbsp;The Company received gross and net proceeds of approximately&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="6x5" data-tblname="723595" data-tblv="20" id="led723595F20256171752777825335">$4,620,000</a> and <a data-tblloc="6x8" data-tblname="723595" data-tblv="20" id="led723595F20256171752777840077">$4,251,000</a>, respectively, related to the exercise of the Preferred and Common Warrants.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 16pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;">As of&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="0x1" data-tblname="723164" data-tblv="20" id="led723164F20256171752777926698">July 15, 2025</a>, we had: i)&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="0x2" data-tblname="723164" data-tblv="20" id="led723164F20256171752777938091">1,914,627</a> shares of Common Stock issued and outstanding, ii)&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="1x1" data-tblname="723165" data-tblv="20" id="led723165F20256171752778238389">200</a> Preferred Shares and&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x1" data-tblname="723165" data-tblv="20" id="led723165F20256171752778248874">30,827</a>&nbsp;Preferred Warrants outstanding, iii)&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="4x1" data-tblname="723165" data-tblv="20" id="led723165F20256171752778258805">1,672,715</a> Common Warrants outstanding, iv)&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="5x1" data-tblname="723165" data-tblv="20" id="led723165F20256171752778268257">1,989,392</a> Pre-Funded Warrants outstanding, v),&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="7x1" data-tblname="723165" data-tblv="20" id="led723165F20256171752778277753">153,470</a> 2023 Placement Agent Warrants outstanding, vi)&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="8x1" data-tblname="723165" data-tblv="20" id="led723165F20256171752778287471">99,470</a> 2025 Placement Agent Warrants outstanding, and vii)&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="10x1" data-tblname="723165" data-tblv="20" id="led723165F20256171752778299987">100,000</a> Advisor&nbsp;Warrants outstanding.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;text-align:justify;margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt;text-indent:45pt;">The shares of Common Stock issuable upon the conversion of the Preferred Shares are herein referred to as &#8220;Conversion Shares,&#8221; the shares of Common Stock issuable upon the exercise of the Supplement Warrants are herein referred to&nbsp;as "Supplement Warrant Shares," the shares of Common Stock issuable upon the exercise of the Common Warrants are herein referred to as &#8220;Warrant Common Shares,&#8221; the shares of&nbsp; Common Stock issuable upon the exercise of the Pre-Funded Warrants are herein referred to as &#8220;Pre-Funded Warrant Shares,&#8221; the shares of&nbsp; Common Stock issuable upon the exercise of the 2025 Placement Agent Warrants are herein referred to as &#8220;Placement Agent Warrant Shares,&#8221; and the shares of&nbsp; Common Stock issuable upon the exercise of the Advisor Warrants are herein referred to as &#8220;Advisor Warrant Shares&#8221; (and, together with the Warrant Common Shares, the Supplement Warrant Shares, the Pre-Funded Warrant Shares and the Placement Agent Warrant Shares, as &#8220;Warrant Shares&#8221;).</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;">We are registering i)&nbsp;the resale of the Warrant Common Shares, Conversion Shares, and Supplement Warrant Shares covered by this prospectus as required by the Registration Rights Agreement, dated March 30, 2023, by and among the Company and the Investors, as amended or waived (the &#8220;Registration Rights Agreement&#8221;), ii) the resale of the Pre-Funded Warrants Shares&nbsp;pursuant to the terms of the 2025 Purchase Agreement, and iii) the resale of&nbsp;the 2025 Placement Agent Warrant Shares&nbsp;and Advisor&nbsp;Warrant Shares. We previously registered 6,550 Preferred Shares, 32,750 Warrant Preferred Shares and 300,013&nbsp;shares of our Common Stock issuable upon the conversion of shares of Series F Preferred Stock on the Registration Statement on Form S-3 (Reg. No. 333-272094) declared effective by the SEC on June 20, 2023. We also previously registered 95,772&nbsp;shares of our Common Stock underlying Common Warrants, 225,000 shares of our Common Stock underlying the Preferred Shares and 900,000 shares of our Common Stock underlying Preferred Shares issuable upon exercise of Preferred Warrants on the Registration Statement on Form S-3 (Reg. No. 333-276322) declared effective by the SEC on January 16, 2024. We also previously registered 1,373,930 shares of our Common Stock underlying Common Warrants and 153,470 shares of our Common Stock underlying 2023 Placement Agent Warrants issued in connection with the 2023 Purchase Agreement&nbsp;on the Registration statement on Form S-3 (Reg No. 333-282515) declared effective by the SEC on October 16, 2024. The selling stockholders will receive all of the proceeds from any sales of the shares offered hereby. We will not receive any of the proceeds, but we will incur expenses in connection with the offering. To the extent the Common Warrants and/or Preferred Warrants are exercised for cash, if at all, we will receive the exercise price of the Common Warrants and/or Preferred Warrants. As of&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="0x1" data-tblname="723164" data-tblv="20" id="led723164F20256171752777926698">July 15, 2025</a>, we have received gross proceeds of&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="1x5" data-tblname="723595" data-tblv="20" id="led723595F20256171752778385884">$1,875,000</a> and&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="0x5" data-tblname="723595" data-tblv="20" id="led723595F20256171752778398289">$2,745,000</a> from the exercise of&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="1x1" data-tblname="723595" data-tblv="20" id="led723595F20256171752778411787">1,923</a> Preferred Warrants and&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="3x1" data-tblname="723595" data-tblv="20" id="led723595F20256171752778422323">804,959</a> Common Warrants, respectively.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-indent: 45pt; text-align: justify;">The selling stockholders may sell these shares through public or private transactions at market prices prevailing at the time of sale or at negotiated prices. The timing and amount of any sale are within the sole discretion of the selling stockholders. Our registration of the Warrant Common Shares,&nbsp;Conversion Shares, and Supplement Warrant Shares covered by this prospectus does not mean that the selling stockholders will offer or sell any of the shares. For further information regarding the possible methods by which the Pre-Funded Warrant Shares, the Warrant Common Shares, the Placement Agent Warrant Shares, the Advisor&nbsp;Warrant Shares, the Supplement Warrant Shares, and the Conversion Shares may be distributed, see &#8220;Plan of Distribution&#8221; beginning on page 32&nbsp;of this prospectus.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 9pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;">Our Common Stock is listed on the Nasdaq Capital Market under the symbol &#8220;OBLG.&#8221;&nbsp;On <a data-tblloc="0x1" data-tblname="723164" data-tblv="20" id="led723164F20256151752598381671">July 15, 2025</a>, the last reported sale price of our Common Stock on the Nasdaq Capital Market was <a data-tblloc="0x6" data-tblname="723164" data-tblv="20" id="led723164F20256151752598399575">$4.39</a>&nbsp;per share.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;"><b>Investing in our securities involves a high degree of risk. You should review carefully the risks and uncertainties described under the heading </b>&#8220;<b>Risk Factors</b>&#8221;<b> on page 10&nbsp;of this prospectus, and under similar headings in the other documents that are incorporated by reference into this prospectus, each of which describes specific risks and other information that should be considered before you make an investment decision.</b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;"><b>Neither the Securities and Exchange Commission nor any state securities commission has approved or disapproved of these securities or determined if this prospectus is truthful or complete. Any representation to the contrary is a criminal offense.</b></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;text-align:center;margin:0pt;"><b><a id="about" name="about" title="about"></a>ABOUT THIS PROSPECTUS</b></p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;">Unless the context requires otherwise or unless otherwise noted, all references in this prospectus to &#8220;<i>our company</i>,&#8221; &#8220;<i>we</i>,&#8221; &#8220;<i>our</i>,&#8221; &#8220;<i>Oblong</i>&#8221; and &#8220;<i>us</i>&#8221; refer to Oblong, Inc. and its subsidiaries, and all references to the &#8220;<i>Selling Stockholders</i>&#8221; refer to those selling stockholders identified in this prospectus. Also, any reference to &#8220;<i>common share</i>&#8221; or &#8220;<i>Common Stock</i>&#8221; refers to our Common Stock, $0.0001 par value per share (the &#8220;Common Stock&#8221;).</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;">This prospectus is part of a registration statement on Form S-3 that we filed with the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission (the &#8220;SEC&#8221;), utilizing a &#8220;shelf&#8221; registration process. Under this shelf registration process, the Selling Stockholders identified herein may sell or otherwise dispose of up to an aggregate of up to&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="11x5" data-tblname="723165" data-tblv="20" id="led723165F20256171752778506020">4,178,249</a> shares of our Common Stock issuable to them upon exercise of the Common Warrants, Pre-Funded Warrants, Placement Agent Warrants, Advisor&nbsp;Warrants, and Supplement Warrants,&nbsp;and issuable to them upon the conversion of the Series F Preferred Stock.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;">We urge you to read carefully this prospectus (as supplemented and amended), together with the information incorporated herein by reference as described under the heading &#8220;Where You Can Find More Information&#8221; before deciding whether to invest in any of the Common Stock being offered hereby. This prospectus contains summaries of certain provisions contained in some of the documents described herein, but reference should be made to the actual documents for complete information. All of the summaries are qualified in their entirety by the actual documents. Copies of some of the documents referred to herein have been filed, will be filed or will be incorporated by reference as exhibits to the registration statement of which this prospectus is a part, and you may obtain copies of those documents as described below under the section entitled &#8220;Where You Can Find More Information.&#8221;</p>

<div contenteditable="false" data-applyto="t" data-auto-pgnum="start" data-displaynum="1" data-fontname="Times New Roman" data-fontsize="10pt" data-numstyle="a" data-prefix="" data-startnum="1" data-suffix="" data-textalign="center">&nbsp;</div>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;text-align:center;margin:0pt;"><b><a id="oblong" name="oblong" title="oblong"></a>OBLONG, INC.</b></p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;"><i>This summary description about us and our business highlights selected information contained elsewhere in this prospectus or incorporated by reference into this prospectus. It does not contain all the information you should consider before investing in our securities. Important information is incorporated by reference into this prospectus. To understand this offering fully, you should read carefully the entire prospectus, including </i>&#8220;<i>Risk Factors</i>&#8221;<i> and </i>&#8220;<i>Cautionary Statement Regarding Forward-Looking Statements,</i>&#8221;<i> together with the additional information described under </i>&#8220;<i>Information Incorporated by Reference.</i>&#8221;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-align: justify;"><b>Overview</b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 7pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;">Oblong provides innovative video collaboration and network solutions, centered around our patented Mezzanine&#8482; product line and managed services. Mezzanine&#8482; enables dynamic, multi-user visual collaboration across screens, devices, and locations, enhancing virtual meetings, presentations, and productivity. Our offerings include the Mezzanine&#8482; 200, 300, and 600 Series (two to six screens) with maintenance contracts, alongside subscription-based network and video collaboration services ensuring secure, high-quality connectivity and user-friendly experiences.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 7pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;">In recent years, the Company&nbsp;has faced declining revenues due to the COVID-19 pandemic&#8217;s impact on traditional office environments and reduced demand for Mezzanine&#8482; and managed services. This prompted a strategic review to address market shifts, manage costs, and drive sustainable growth recognizing that revitalizing the business likely required additional capital for product development, marketing, and sales to meet evolving customer needs.</p>

<p style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-align: justify;"><b>Strategy</b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 5pt; text-indent: 45pt; text-align: justify;">On June 6, 2025, we entered into the 2025 Securities Purchase Agreement, dated as of June 5, 2025, with certain accredited investors, pursuant to which we issued and sold, in the 2025 Private Placement, Pre-Funded Warrants to acquire up to 1,989,392 shares of our Common Stock in exchange for gross proceeds of approximately $7.5 million. In conjunction with this financing, the Company will begin to migrate its&#8217; product focus from Mezzanine and related services to the AI and digital assets market.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 5pt; text-indent: 45pt; text-align: justify;">Oblong envisions a dynamic integration into the Bittensor ecosystem, embracing its decentralized AI network to build a thriving and sustainable future. By staking $TAO tokens within Bittensor&#8217;s framework, the Company seeks to create a robust foundation that could fuel long-term growth and engagement, focusing on internal initiatives and collaborative partnerships to amplify its impact in the decentralized AI landscape.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 36pt;">The Company aims to act as a central catalyst, uniting community engagement, user empowerment, and technical expertise within subnets. It seeks to foster collaboration through vibrant spaces for knowledge-sharing, equip users with intuitive tools to seamlessly explore the ecosystem, and contribute operational insights to enhance decentralized AI. By harmonizing these efforts, Oblong hopes to spark innovation, deepen connections across Bittensor&#8217;s network, and become a tangible contributor in shaping the future of decentralized intelligence, creating an inclusive environment where creativity and participation thrive.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<div class="PGBK" style="width: 100%; margin-left: 0pt; margin-right: 0pt">
<div class="PGNUM" data-number="1" data-prefix="" data-suffix="" style="text-align: center; width: 100%; font-size: 10pt; font-family: Times New Roman;">1</div>

<hr style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always; border: none; width: 100%; height: 2px; color: #000000; background-color: #000000">
<div class="PGHDR" style="text-align: left; width: 100%">
<div class="hf-row">
<div class="TOCLink hf-cell" style="width: 100%; display: inline-block; text-align: left;"><a href="#toc" style="font-weight: initial; font-style: initial; font-variant: initial; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt;">Table of Contents</a></div>
</div>
</div>
</div>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;"><b>2023 Private Placement of Preferred Shares and Warrants</b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;">On March 30, 2023, we entered into the 2023 Purchase Agreement with certain accredited investors, pursuant to which we issued and sold,&nbsp;in&nbsp;the 2023 Private Placement, an aggregate of (i) 6,550 Preferred Shares, (ii) Preferred Warrants to acquire up to 32,750 Warrant Preferred Shares and (iii) Common Warrants to acquire up to 1,918,371 shares of Common Stock, all in exchange for gross proceeds of approximately $6.4 million. The Common Warrants issued in connection with the 2023 Private Placement included 153,470 2023 Placement Agent Warrants issued to our placement agent in consideration for services provided thereto. The terms of the Preferred Shares are as set forth in the Certificate of Designations of Series F Preferred Stock of Oblong, Inc. (the &#8220;Certificate of Designations&#8221;), which was filed and became effective with the Secretary of State of the State of Delaware on March 31, 2023. The Preferred Warrants were immediately exercisable and expire three years from issuance and the Common Warrants became exercisable on October 1, 2023, six months and one day after issuance (the &#8220;Initial Exercisability Date&#8221;) and expire five years from the Initial Exercisability Date.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;">In connection with the 2023 Private Placement, we entered into the Registration Rights Agreement, as amended by those certain waivers and amendments dated as of April 14, 2023, May 18, 2023 and August 15, 2023, pursuant to which we were obligated, among other things, to file an initial registration statement (the &#8220;Initial Registration Statement&#8221;) with the SEC no later than the tenth Business Day after the Stockholder Approval Date (as defined in the Purchase Agreement), registering for the resale by the selling stockholders of the Preferred Shares, the Warrant Preferred Shares, the Warrant Common Shares and the Conversion Shares, provided that in the Initial Registration Statement with respect to the Preferred Shares, the Warrant Preferred Shares and the Conversion Shares, we were only required to register (i) an amount of Series F Preferred Stock equal to 100% of the sum of (w) the shares of Series F Preferred Stock outstanding and (x) the maximum number of shares of Series F Preferred Stock issuable upon exercise of the Preferred Warrants outstanding, and (ii) 300,000 Conversion Shares issuable upon conversion of the Preferred Shares outstanding, subject to certain assumptions set forth in the Registration Rights Agreement. On May 9, 2023, we filed the Initial Registration Statement with the SEC. The SEC declared the Initial Registration Statement effective on June 20, 2023. We will use our best efforts to maintain the Initial Registration Statement effective until the earlier of (x) the date on which the selling stockholders may sell their Conversion Shares or Warrant Common Shares without restriction pursuant to Rule 144 under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended (the &#8220;Securities Act&#8221;), and (y) the date on which the selling stockholders no longer hold any Conversion Shares or Warrant Common Shares.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;">Unless waived, accelerated or delayed by certain holders of the securities issued in the 2023 Private Placement, the 2023 Purchase Agreement&nbsp;required the Company to file a second resale registration statement (the &#8220;Second Registration Statement&#8221;) covering the resale of, to the extent not covered by the Initial Registration Statement, (i) 100% of the sum of (x) the Preferred Shares outstanding as of such date and (y) the maximum number of the Series F Preferred Stock issuable upon exercise of the Preferred Warrants outstanding as of such date, (ii) 100% of the maximum number of Warrant Common Shares issuable upon exercise of the Common Warrants (without taking in to account any limitations on exercise set forth therein) and (iii) 100% of the maximum number of Conversion Shares issuable upon conversion of the Preferred Shares, subject to certain assumptions set forth in the Registration Rights Agreement.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;">On April 14, 2023, the Required Holders (as defined in the Purchase Agreement) waived certain terms of the Transaction Documents, including the requirement to authorize, reserve and register shares of the Company&#8217;s Common Stock in an amount more than currently authorized and available, and extended the deadline for the Company&#8217;s filing of resale registration statements.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;">On May 18, 2023, the Required Holders (as defined in the Purchase Agreement) amended the Registration Rights Agreement to provide that the Company was required to register on the Initial Registration Statement (i) an amount of Series F Preferred Stock equal to 100% of the sum of (w) the shares of Series F Preferred Stock outstanding and (x) the maximum number of shares of Series F Preferred Stock issuable upon exercise of the Preferred Warrants outstanding, and (ii) 300,000 Conversion Shares issuable upon conversion of the Preferred Shares outstanding, subject to certain assumptions set forth in the Registration Rights Agreement.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;">Effective August 15, 2023, the Required Holders (as defined in the Purchase Agreement) extended the filing deadline of the Second Registration Statement to a time to be agreed upon between the Company and the Required Holders.&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;">On December 29, 2023, we filed the Second Registration Statement covering the resale of (i) 95,772 shares of our Common Stock underlying Common Warrants, (ii) 225,000 shares of our Common Stock underlying the Preferred Shares, and (iii) 900,000 shares of our Common Stock underlying the Preferred Shares issuable upon exercise of Preferred Warrants. The SEC declared the Second Registration Statement effective on January 16, 2024.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 10pt; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 9pt; text-align: left; text-indent: 36pt;">On October 4, 2024, we filed a third Registration Statement covering the resale of 1,373,930 shares of our Common Stock issuable upon exercise of the Common Warrants and upon the conversion of shares of Series F Preferred Stock and 153,470 shares of our Common Stock issuable upon the exercise of the 2023 Placement Agent Warrants. The SEC declared the Third Registration Statement effective on October 16, 2024.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-align: justify;"><b>2025 Private Placement of Pre-Funded Warrants</b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;">On June 6, 2025, we entered into the 2025&nbsp;Securities Purchase Agreement, dated as of June 5, 2025, with certain accredited investors, pursuant to which we issued and sold, in the 2025 Private Placement, Pre-Funded Warrants&nbsp;to acquire up to 1,989,392 shares of our Common Stock in exchange for gross proceeds of approximately $7.5 million. In connection with the 2025 Private Placement, we also issued the 2025 Placement Agent Warrants&nbsp;to acquire up to 99,470&nbsp;shares of our Common Stock, and Advisor&nbsp;Warrants to purchase up to 100,000 shares of our Common Stock. We were required pursuant to the terms of the 2025 Purchase Agreement to file a registration statement registering the shares of Common Stock issuable upon the exercise of the Pre-Funded Warrants within 15 days of the date of the 2025 Purchase Agreement.</p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 9pt; text-align: justify;"><b><i>Preferred Shares</i></b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;">The terms of the Preferred Shares are as set forth in the Certificate of Designations which was filed with and became effective with the Secretary of State for the State of Delaware on March 30, 2023, as amended or waived. The Certificate of Designations was filed as Exhibit 3.1 to the Company&#8217;s Current Report on Form 8-K, filed with the SEC on April 3, 2023, and is incorporated herein by reference. On October 6, 2023, the Company and investors holding a majority of the outstanding Preferred Shares (the "Requisite Preferred Holders") agreed to waive any and all provisions, terms, covenants and obligations in the Certificate of Designations to the extent such provisions permit the conversion of the Preferred Shares to occur under the alternate conversion mechanism at a price below $11.168 (the &#8220;Waiver&#8221;). Pursuant to the Waiver, the Company and the Requisite Preferred Holders agreed that notwithstanding&nbsp;anything to the contrary in the Certificate of Designations, each of the &#8220;Alternate Conversion Price&#8221; and the &#8220;Floor Price&#8221; as set forth in the Certificate of Designations shall in no event be less than $11.168 (as adjusted for stock splits, stock dividends, stock combinations, recapitalizations and similar events). The Waiver was filed as Exhibit 10.1 to the Company&#8217;s Current Report on Form 8-K, filed with the SEC on October 10, 2023, and is incorporated herein by reference.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;">The Preferred Shares are convertible into fully paid and non-assessable shares of the Company&#8217;s Common Stock at the election of the holder at any time.&nbsp;Following the 2025 Private Placement, in accordance with the terms of the Certificate of Designations, the Conversion Price was adjusted to $3.77 per share. The holders of the Preferred Shares may also elect to convert their Preferred Shares at an alternative conversion price equal to the lower of (i) 80% of the applicable Conversion Price as in effect on the date of the conversion, (ii) 80% of the closing price on the trading day immediately preceding the delivery of the conversion notice, and (iii) the greater of (a) the Floor Price (as defined in the Certificate of Designations) and (b) the quotient of (x) the sum of the five lowest Closing Bid Prices (as defined in the Certificate of Designations) for trading days in the 30 consecutive trading day period ending and including the trading day immediately preceding the delivery of the applicable Conversion Notice, divided by (y) five; provided that the conversion of the Preferred Shares under this alternative conversion mechanism&nbsp;shall under no circumstance occur at a price below $3.77.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<div class="PGBK" style="width: 100%; margin-left: 0pt; margin-right: 0pt">
<div class="PGFTR" style="text-align: center; width: 100%">
<div class="hf-row">
<div class="hf-cell PGNUM" data-number="3" data-prefix="" data-suffix="" style="text-align: center; font-size: 10pt; font-family: Times New Roman;">3</div>

<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 10pt; margin: 0pt; text-align: left">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;">The holders of the Preferred Shares are entitled to dividends of 9% per annum, which is payable in arrears quarterly. The initial stated value of the Preferred Shares is $1,000 (the &#8220;Stated Value&#8221;). Accrued dividends may be paid, at our option, in cash and if not paid, shall increase the Stated Value of the Preferred Shares. Upon the occurrence and during the continuance of a Triggering Event (as defined in the Certificate of Designations), the Preferred Shares will accrue dividends at the rate of 20% per annum (the &#8220;Default Rate&#8221;). Additionally, the Default Rate will be triggered in the event that the Company is prohibited from issuing shares of Common Stock to a buyer upon any conversion due to the failure by the Company to have sufficient shares of Common Stock available out of the authorized but unissued shares of Common Stock until such time as the Company cures the authorized share failure. The Preferred Shares have no voting rights, other than with respect to certain matters affecting the rights of the Preferred Shares. On matters with respect to which the holders of the Preferred Shares have a right to vote, holders of the Preferred Shares will have voting rights on an as-converted basis to Common Stock.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;">Our ability to settle conversions is subject to certain limitations set forth in the Certificate of Designations and our ability to settle exercise of the Warrants is subject to certain limitations. Further, the Certificate of Designations contains a certain beneficial ownership limitation after giving effect to the issuance of shares of Common Stock issuable upon conversion of the Preferred Shares.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;">The Certificate of Designations includes certain Triggering Events (as defined in the Certificate of Designations), including, among other things, (i) the failure to file and maintain an effective registration statement covering the sale of the holder&#8217;s securities registrable pursuant to the Registration Rights Agreement, (ii) the failure to pay any amounts due to the holders of the Preferred Shares when due, and (iii) if Peter Holst ceases to be the chief executive officer of the Company other than because of his death and a qualified replacement, reasonably acceptable to a majority of the holders of the Preferred Shares, is not appointed within thirty (30) business days. In connection with a Triggering Event, the Default Rate is triggered.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;">We are subject to certain affirmative and negative covenants regarding the incurrence of indebtedness, acquisition transactions, the existence of liens, the repayment of indebtedness, the payment of cash in respect of dividends (other than dividends pursuant to the Certificate of Designations), maintenance of properties and restriction on the transfer of assets, among other matters.&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;text-indent:36pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 9pt; text-align: justify;"><b><i>Warrants</i></b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-align: justify;"><i>Preferred Warrants</i></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;">The Preferred Warrants are immediately exercisable for shares of our Series F Preferred Stock at an exercise price of $975. The exercise price is subject to customary adjustments for stock dividends, stock combinations, stock splits, recapitalizations and the like, and subject to price-based adjustment, on a full ratchet basis, in the event of any issuances of Common Stock, or securities convertible, exercisable or exchangeable for Common Stock, at a price below the then-applicable exercise price (subject to certain exceptions). The Preferred Warrants expire three years from the date of issuance and are exercisable for cash. Under the terms of the Preferred Warrant, the Company is restricted from entering into a merger, business combination, sale of all or substantially all of its assets or similar transaction (&#8220;Fundamental Transaction&#8221;) unless the successor entity is a publicly traded company and assumes all of the Company&#8217;s obligations under the Transaction Documents (as defined in the Purchase Agreement). In the event of a Fundamental Transaction, the Company or its successor entity, at their sole option, may purchase the Preferred Warrants by paying to the warrant holders an amount of cash (subject to certain exceptions) equal to the Black Scholes Value (as defined in the Preferred Warrant) of the remaining unexercised portion of the Warrants on the date of consummation of the Fundamental Transaction, provided, however, that, if the Fundamental Transaction is not within the Company&#8217;s control, the holder shall only be entitled to receive from the Company or any successor entity the same type of consideration which the holder would have been entitled to receive upon the happening of the applicable Fundamental Transaction had the Preferred Warrant been completely exercised (and the underlying Warrant Preferred Shares completely converted) immediately prior to the applicable Fundamental Transaction, at the Black Scholes Value of the unexercised portion of the Warrant, that is being offered and paid to the holders of Common Stock of the Company in connection with the Fundamental Transaction. Notwithstanding the foregoing, any payment of cash in accordance with the foregoing shall not be permitted to be made from the Company&#8217;s cash balance upon the date of the consummation of the Fundamental Transaction and may only be paid by the successor entity or from the proceeds of a capital raise that would be accounted for as permanent equity on either the Company&#8217;s or successor entity&#8217;s balance sheet.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;">Upon exercise of a Preferred Warrant, in addition to the Series F Preferred Stock, the holder&nbsp;shall receive Common Warrants to purchase a number of shares of Common Stock equal to 100% of the number of shares of Common Stock the Investors would receive if the Series F Preferred Shares issuable upon exercise of such Warrant were converted at the applicable Conversion Price.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-align: justify;"><i>Common Warrants</i></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;">The Common Warrants, prior to the Reverse Stock Split, were exercisable for shares of Common Stock at an exercise price of $1.71 per share, beginning on or after the sixth month and one day anniversary after the issuance date and expiring five and a half years after the date of issuance. The exercise price is subject to customary adjustments for stock dividends, stock combinations (including the Reverse Stock Split), stock splits, recapitalizations and the like, and subject to price-based adjustment, on a full ratchet basis, in the event of any issuances of Common Stock, or securities convertible, exercisable or exchangeable for Common Stock, at a price below the then-applicable exercise price (subject to certain exceptions).&nbsp; Following the Reverse Stock Split, in accordance with the terms of the Common Warrants, the exercise price of the Common Warrants was adjusted to $3.41438 per share. The Common Warrants are exercisable for cash, provided that if there is no effective registration statement available permitting the resale of the Warrant Common Shares, the Common Warrants may be exercised on a cashless basis. Under the terms of the Common Warrant, the Company is restricted from entering into a Fundamental Transaction unless the successor entity is a publicly traded company and assumes all of the Company&#8217;s obligations under the Transaction Documents. In the event of a Fundamental Transaction, the Company or its successor entity, at their sole option, may purchase the Common Warrants by paying to the warrant holders an amount of cash (subject to certain exceptions) equal to the Black Scholes Value (as defined in the Common Warrant) of the remaining unexercised portion of the Warrants on the date of consummation of the Fundamental Transaction, provided, however, that, if the Fundamental Transaction is not within the Company&#8217;s control, the holder shall only be entitled to receive from the Company or any successor entity the same type of consideration which the holder would have been entitled to receive upon the happening of the applicable Fundamental Transaction had the Common Warrant been completely exercised immediately prior to the applicable Fundamental Transaction, at the Black Scholes Value of the unexercised portion of the Warrant, that is being offered and paid to the holders of Common Stock of the Company in connection with the Fundamental Transaction. Notwithstanding the foregoing, any payment of cash in accordance with the foregoing shall not be permitted to be made from the Company&#8217;s cash balance upon the date of the consummation of the Fundamental Transaction and may only be paid by the successor entity or from the proceeds of a capital raise that would be accounted for as permanent equity on either the Company&#8217;s or successor entity&#8217;s balance sheet.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 10pt; margin: 0pt; text-align: left">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 16pt; text-indent: -9pt; text-align: justify;"><i>Supplement Warrants</i></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 16pt; text-indent: -9pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 16pt; text-indent: 27pt; text-align: justify;">The terms of the Supplement Warrants are identical to the those of the Common Warrants, as adjusted, amended, or waived as of the date of issuance of such Supplement Warrants.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 16pt; text-indent: -9pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 16pt; text-indent: -9pt; text-align: justify;"><i>Pre-Funded Warrants</i></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 7pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;">The material terms and provisions of the Pre-Funded Warrants to purchase shares of Common Stock are summarized below. This summary is subject to and qualified in its entirety by the form of pre-funded warrant, which was filed with the SEC as an exhibit to our Current Report on Form 8-K on June 6, 2025.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;text-indent:36pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 7pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;"><i>Exercise Price</i>. The exercise price upon exercise of each Pre-Funded Warrant is $0.0001 per share of Common Stock, with an aggregate exercise price of $3.77 per share of Common Stock, of which $3.7699 per share of Common Stock was paid by the holders at the closing on June 10, 2025. The exercise price of the Pre-Funded Warrants is subject to appropriate adjustment in the event of stock dividends, subdivisions, stock splits, stock combinations, cash distributions, reclassifications, exchanges, combinations or substitutions affecting our Common Stock.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 7pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;"><i>Payment of Exercise Price</i>. The Pre-Funded Warrant holders have the option to provide payment of the exercise price of the shares being acquired upon exercise of the Pre-Funded Warrants (i) by payment of the aggregate exercise price to us or (ii) by cashless exercise.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 7pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;"><i>Cashless Exercise</i>. In lieu of making the cash payment otherwise contemplated to be made to us upon such exercise in payment of the aggregate exercise price, the holders of Pre-Funded Warrants may elect instead to receive upon such exercise the net number of shares of Common Stock determined according to a formula set forth in the Pre-Funded Warrants.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 7pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;"><i>Transferability</i>. Subject to applicable laws and the restriction on transfer set forth in the Pre-Funded Warrants, the Pre-Funded Warrants may be transferred.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 7pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;"><i>Fundamental Transactions</i>. Upon the consummation of a fundamental transaction (as described in the Pre-Funded Warrants, and generally including any reorganization, recapitalization or reclassification of our common stock, the sale, transfer or other disposition of all or substantially all of our assets, our consolidation or merger with or into another person in which we are not the surviving entity, the acquisition of more than 50% of our outstanding common stock, or any person or group becoming the beneficial owner of 50% of the voting power of our outstanding common stock), a holder of the Pre-Funded Warrants will be entitled to receive, upon exercise of the Pre-Funded Warrants, the same kind and amount of securities, cash or other property that such holder would have received had they exercised the Pre-Funded Warrants immediately prior to such fundamental transaction, without regard to any limitations on exercise contained in the Pre-Funded Warrants.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 7pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;"><i>Rights as a Stockholder</i>. Except for the right to participate in certain dividends and distributions and as otherwise provided in the Pre-Funded Warrants or by virtue of a holder&#8217;s ownership of our Common Stock, the holders of the Pre-Funded Warrants do not have the rights or privileges of holders of our Common Stock, including any voting rights, until they exercise their Pre-Funded Warrants.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 7pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;"><i>Waivers and Amendments</i>. No term of the Pre-Funded Warrants may be amended or waived without the written consent of the holder of such Pre-Funded Warrants.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 16pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 7pt; text-indent: 0pt; text-align: justify;"><i>2025 Placement Agent Warrants</i></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 16pt; text-indent: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 7pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;">The material terms and provisions of the Placement Agent Warrants to purchase shares of Common Stock are summarized below. This summary is subject to and qualified in its entirety by the form of placement agent warrant, which was filed with the SEC as an exhibit to our Current Report on Form 8-K on June 6, 2025.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 16pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;">The terms of the 2025 Placement Agent Warrants are substantially the same as those of the Pre-Funded Warrants, except that the 2025 Placement Agent Warrants will expire on June 10, 2030, are initially exercisable at a price of $4.7125 per share of Common Stock, may only be exercised a cashless basis if there is no effective registration statement registering the underlying shares, and in the event of a Fundamental Transaction as defined in the 2025 Placement Agent Warrants, warrant holders may require the company to purchase the remaining unexercised portion of a 2025 Placement Agent Warrant for an amount equal to the Black-Scholes Value of that portion, as of the date of the Fundamental Transaction, unless the Fundamental Transaction is not within the Company&#8217;s control, as described in the 2025 Placement Agent Warrants. There is no established public trading market for the 2025 Placement Agent Warrants and we do not intend to list the 2025 Placement Agent Warrants on any national securities exchange or nationally recognized trading system.&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 17pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 7pt; text-indent: 0pt; text-align: justify;"><i>Advisor Warrants</i></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 16pt; text-indent: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 7pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;">The material terms and provisions of the Advisor&nbsp;Warrants to purchase shares of Common Stock are summarized below. This summary is subject to and qualified in its entirety by the form of Advisor Warrant, filed herewith and incorporated by reference herein.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 16pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 7pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;">The terms of the Advisor Warrants are substantially the same as those of the 2025 Placement Agent Warrants, except that the Advisor Warrants will expire on June 5,2028, are initially exercisable in part beginning on July 7, 2025 at a price of $3.77 per share of Common Stock, and will vest in equal installments at a rate of 1/12th (8.33%) per month, beginning on the thirty day anniversary of the issue date, for twelve months.</p>

You should read these risks before you invest in our securities. We may be unable, for many reasons, including those that are beyond our control, to implement our business strategy.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: center;"><b><a id="risk" name="risk" title="risk"></a>RISK FACTORS</b></p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;"><i>Investing in our securities involves a high degree of risk. You should carefully review the risks and uncertainties described below, as well as the other information contained or incorporated by reference in this prospectus, including information in our most recent Annual Report on Form 10-K, as revised or supplemented by our Quarterly Reports on Form 10-Q and Current Reports on Form 8-K filed with the SEC since the filing of our most recent Annual Report on Form 10-K, each of which are on file with the SEC and are incorporated by reference in this prospectus. The occurrence of any of these risks might cause you to lose all or part of your investment in the offered securities. The risks described below are not the only ones facing our company. Additional risks and uncertainties not currently known to us or that we currently deem to be immaterial may also materially and adversely affect our business or results of operations in the future. Any of the following risks could materially adversely affect our business, financial condition or results of operations. In such case, you may lose all or part of your original investment in the securities offered by the selling stockholders hereby.</i></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-align: justify;"><b><i>The issuance of the securities in the 2023 Private Placement and the 2025&nbsp;Private Placement significantly diluted the ownership interest of the existing holders of our Common Stock, and the market price of our Common Stock will likely decline significantly as a result of sales of such securities into the public market by the selling stockholders and subsequent investors or the perception that such sales may occur.</i></b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;">Our existing holders of Common Stock have been significantly diluted by the issuance of the securities in the 2023 Private Placement, and would be subject to additional dilution as a result of the conversion of those securities and the securities issued in the 2025 Private Placement into shares of Common Stock. Our public float was significantly increased and the market price of our Common Stock could decline significantly as a result of subsequent sales of the shares of Common Stock issued, or underlying the securities issued&nbsp;in the 2023 Private Placement and the 2025 Private Placement, which could occur at any time, or the perception that such sales may occur. As of July 15, 2025, we had <a data-tblloc="0x2" data-tblname="723164" data-tblv="20" id="led723164F20256151752599156059">1,914,627</a>&nbsp;shares of Common Stock issued and outstanding and <a data-tblloc="1x1" data-tblname="723165" data-tblv="20" id="led723165F20256151752601444149">200</a>&nbsp;Preferred Shares outstanding.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;">In addition, the exercise price or conversion price of these securities may be at prices below the current and/or then trading prices of shares of our Common Stock or at prices below the price at which our existing shareholders purchased our Common Stock. The selling stockholders may potentially make a significant profit with the resale of the securities depending on the trading price of our securities at the time of a sale and the purchase price of such securities by them. While the selling stockholders may experience a positive rate of return based on the trading price of our securities, the existing holders of our Common Stock may not experience a similar rate of return on the shares of Common Stock they purchased due to differences in the applicable purchase price and trading price.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-align: justify;"><b><i>Future issuances of equity or debt securities by us may adversely affect the market price of our Common Stock.</i></b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;">Our authorized share capital consists of&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="18x1" data-tblname="723165" data-tblv="20" id="led723165F20256151752601488852">150 million</a> shares of Common Stock. As of July 15, 2025, we had an aggregate of approximately&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="19x1" data-tblname="723165" data-tblv="20" id="led723165F20256151752601477666">148.1 million</a>&nbsp;shares of Common Stock authorized but unissued, and approximately <a data-tblloc="20x1" data-tblname="723165" data-tblv="20" id="led723165F20256151752601498924">20.4 million</a>&nbsp;shares of Common Stock reserved but unissued after giving effect to the exercise or conversion, as applicable, of the securities issued in the 2023 Private Placement and the 2025 Private Placement and outstanding awards, assuming <p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 10pt; margin: 0pt; text-align: left">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;">In the future, we may attempt to obtain financing or to increase further our capital resources, or refinance existing obligations, by issuing additional shares of our Common Stock or offering debt or other equity securities, including commercial paper, medium-term notes, senior or subordinated notes, debt securities convertible into equity or shares of preferred stock. Future acquisitions could require substantial additional capital in excess of cash from operations. There can be no guarantee that these offers to exchange will be successful. In addition, we also expect to issue additional shares in connection with exercise of our stock options under our incentive plans.</p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;">Issuing additional shares of our Common Stock or other equity securities or securities convertible into equity for financing or in connection with our incentive plans, acquisitions or otherwise may dilute the economic and voting rights of our existing shareholders or reduce the market price of our Common Stock or both. Upon liquidation, holders of our debt securities and preferred shares, if issued, and lenders with respect to other borrowings would receive a distribution of our available assets prior to the holders of our Common Stock. Debt securities convertible into equity could be subject to adjustments in the conversion ratio pursuant to which certain events may increase the number of equity securities issuable upon conversion. Preferred shares, if issued, could have a preference with respect to liquidating distributions or a preference with respect to dividend payments that could limit our ability to pay dividends to the holders of our Common Stock. Our decision to issue securities in any future offering will depend on market conditions and other factors beyond our control, which may adversely affect the amount, timing or nature of our future offerings. Thus, holders of our Common Stock bear the risk that our future offerings may reduce the market price of our Common Stock and dilute their stockholdings in us. Additionally, we may be required to secure stockholder approval to authorize additional shares of Common Stock if we desire to issue additional shares of Common Stock or other equity securities or securities convertible into equity.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-align: justify;"><b><i>The market price of our Common Stock could decline due to the large number of outstanding shares of our Common Stock that may become available for future sale.</i></b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;">Sales of substantial amounts of our Common Stock in the public market in future offerings, including sales relating to the Warrant Shares and&nbsp;Conversion Shares, or the perception that these sales could occur, could cause the market price of our Common Stock to decline. These sales could also make it more difficult for us to sell equity or equity-related securities in the future, at a time and price that we deem appropriate. In addition, the additional sale of our Common Stock by our officers or directors in the public market, or the perception that these sales may occur, could cause the market price of our Common Stock to decline.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;">We may issue shares of our Common Stock or other securities from time to time as consideration for, or to finance, future acquisitions, investments, debt-for-equity exchanges or for other capital needs. We cannot predict the size of future issuances of our shares or the effect, if any, that future sales and issuances of shares would have on the market price of our Common Stock. If any such acquisition or investment is significant, the number of shares of Common Stock or the number or aggregate principal amount, as the case may be, of other securities that we may issue may in turn be substantial and may result in additional dilution to our shareholders. We may also grant registration rights covering shares of our Common Stock or other securities that we may issue in connection with any such acquisitions and investments.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 10pt; margin: 0pt; text-align: left">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-align: justify;"><b><i>We may not be able to comply with all applicable listing requirements or standards of The Nasdaq Capital Market and Nasdaq could delist our Common Stock.</i></b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 36pt;">Our Common Stock is listed on The Nasdaq Capital Market. In order to maintain that listing, we must satisfy minimum financial and other continued listing requirements and standards.</p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;">In the event that we are unable to maintain compliance with Rule 5550(a)(2) and cannot re-establish compliance within the required timeframe, our Common Stock could be delisted from The Nasdaq Capital Market, which could have a material adverse effect on our financial condition, and which would cause the value of our Common Stock to decline. If our Common Stock is not eligible for listing or quotation on another market or exchange, trading of our Common Stock could be conducted in the over-the-counter market or on an electronic bulletin board established for unlisted securities such as the Pink Sheets or the OTC Bulletin Board. In such event, it would become more difficult to dispose of, or obtain accurate price quotations for, our Common Stock, and there would likely be a reduction in our coverage by security analysts and the news media, which could cause the price of our Common Stock to decline further. In addition, it may be difficult for us to raise additional capital if we are not listed on a national securities exchange.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt; text-indent: 36pt; text-align: justify;">While Nasdaq rules do not impose a specific limit on the number of times a listed company may effect a reverse stock split to maintain or regain compliance with Listing Rule 5810(c)(3)(A), Nasdaq has stated that a series of reverse stock splits may undermine investor confidence in securities listed on Nasdaq. Accordingly, Nasdaq may determine that it is not in the public interest to maintain our listing, even if we regain compliance with Listing Rule 5810(c)(3)(A) as a result of any reverse stock split. In addition, under Nasdaq Listing Rule 5810(c)(3)(A)(iv), if a company&#8217;s securities again fail to meet the Bid Price Rule and the company has effected a reverse stock split within the prior one-year period, or has effected one or more reverse stock splits over the prior two-year period with a cumulative ratio of 250 shares or more to one, the company will not be eligible for an automatic 180-day grace compliance period. Instead, the Nasdaq Listing Qualifications Department will immediately issue a delisting determination, unless the company timely appeals the decision to a Hearings Panel. Because we effected a 1-for-40 reverse stock split on August 23, 2024, if we were to fall out of compliance with the Bid Price Rule prior to August 23, 2025, we would not be eligible for an automatic compliance period and would immediately be issued a delisting determination, subject to our right of timely appeal.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>
